The sense “bierkeller” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bierkeller</i>.

</p>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bierkeller</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mostly in reference to Germany</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***bigwig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>bigwig</a> (39785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First arose in the 1730s, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">big</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wig</i>. Formerly, English <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> of authority wore wigs. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>Bigwig</a></i> plays on the idea that <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> authority <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> denoted by a larger wig.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>bigwig</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bigwigs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of importance to a group or organization.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The company <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>bigwig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> gathering his staff together for a meeting today.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b> May 5,  “Reality star <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bethenny_Frankel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bethenny Frankel">Bethenny Frankel</a> talks hats, hangovers and her <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kentucky_Derby" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kentucky Derby">Kentucky Derby</a> party at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_City_Casino" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Empire City Casino">Empire City <a href = vnd.unilang:casino.html>Casino</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_Daily_News" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:New York Daily News">New York Daily News</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Before her hay-day, she attended many derbys under her dad's celebrity where she'd hobnob with the <b>bigwigs</b> in Millionaire's Row.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***bij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> (69)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>at, with
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feest.html>feest</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>With</b> us it's always a party.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>by, close to
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woon.html>woon</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hutje.html>hutje</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I live in a little <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a> <b>by</b> the sea.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to, towards
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>Kom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>Come to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> by, through, by means of, through the action or presence of</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></strong>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bië</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bijō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijen.html>bijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijtje.html>bijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bee, insect of the clade Anthophila</li></ol>

***bijdragen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijdragen.html>bijdragen</a> (9788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dragen.html>dragen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijdragen.html>bijdragen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contribute</li></ol>

***bijeenhouden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijeenhouden.html>bijeenhouden</a> (95189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijeen.html>bijeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijeenhouden.html>bijeenhouden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold together</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bijeenhouden.html>bijeenhouden</a></b>

***bijgeloof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloof</a> (9691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>superstition (a set of unscientific beliefs that future events may be influenced by one's behaviour in some magical or mystical way)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgelovig.html>bijgelovig</a></span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bijgeloof.html>bijgeloof</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***bijhouden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijhouden.html>bijhouden</a> (7546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijhouden.html>bijhouden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep up with (the pace)</li>

***bijt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijt.html>bijt</a> (3164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijt.html>bijt</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">biten</i> (Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">bīt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">byt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijt.html>bijt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijtje.html>bijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a man-made hole in ice <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">on the surface of a body of water</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***bijten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a> (3346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">biten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bītan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bītaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰéydt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>Waarom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gebeten.html>gebeten</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Why <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> you bite <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Blaffende <a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Barking dogs seldom bite. (<i>literally:</i> Barking dogs don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> bite.)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bijzitten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijzitten.html>bijzitten</a> (61633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijzitten.html>bijzitten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sit along, to sit nearby
<ul><li><b>1617</b> April, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Crijnsze, in Hendrik <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jager.html>Jager</a>, "Verweerschrift <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den Contra-Remonstrantschen <a href = vnd.unilang:predikant.html>predikant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Crijnsze, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Brielsche regeering <a href = vnd.unilang:afgezet.html>afgezet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbannen.html>verbannen</a>.", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijdragen.html>Bijdragen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Mededeelingen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>Historisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genootschap.html>Genootschap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 17, published in 1897, page 212.

<li><b>1919</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meester.html>Meester</a>, "Walmende <a href = vnd.unilang:lampen.html>lampen</a>", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>Gids</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 83, issue 3, page 368.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attend
<ul><li><b>1617</b> April, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Crijnsze, in Hendrik <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jager.html>Jager</a>, "Verweerschrift <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den Contra-Remonstrantschen <a href = vnd.unilang:predikant.html>predikant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Crijnsze, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Brielsche regeering <a href = vnd.unilang:afgezet.html>afgezet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbannen.html>verbannen</a>.", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijdragen.html>Bijdragen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Mededeelingen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>Historisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genootschap.html>Genootschap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 17, published in 1897, page 212.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dese.html>Dese</a> besoigne <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> den 27<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em">n</small></small> Septembris <a href = vnd.unilang:anno.html>anno</a> 1616 by <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> handt <a href = vnd.unilang:genomen.html>genomen</a> sijnde, so <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Crijnsse gevraecht, in <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> qualiteyt hy <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> vergaderinge <b>bysitten</b> soude?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be a <a href = vnd.unilang:concubine.html>concubine</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The sense “to sit along/nearby” now mainly appears in the active participle <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijzitten.html>bijzittend</a></i>. The sense “to attend” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now chiefly used with <a href = vnd.unilang:meetings.html>meetings</a> or assemblies as the object. Otherwise this verb <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> replaced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></i> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbij.html>erbij</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> respectively.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijzit.html>bijzit</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijzitster</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijzitter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijzitting</span></li></ul>

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bezonder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besonder</i>. </p>

***bikini.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>bikini</a> (13316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>bikini</a></i>, named after the place name <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>Bikini</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>Bikini</a></i>, the name of the atoll where the United States tested nuclear <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>weapons</a> in July 1946; it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reckoned that the bathing suit would cause as much excitement as a nuclear bomb. This name <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>Bikini</a></i>, the colonial name of the atoll as part of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_New_Guinea" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:German New Guinea">German New Guinea</a>, and this <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marshallese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Marshallese language">Marshallese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mh">Pikinni</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>bikini</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>bikini</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikinietje.html>bikinietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bikini.html>bikini</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:kleding.html>kleding</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zwemmen.html>zwemmen</a>)</span> tweedelige <a href = vnd.unilang:zwemkleding.html>zwemkleding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trok.html>trok</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aandacht.html>aandacht</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bikinietje.html>bikinietje</a></b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bikkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bikkel.html>bikkel</a> (45800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pickel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*bickel</i>, formed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">picken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bicken</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikken.html>bikken</a></i>).
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bickel</i>, older form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pickel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikkel.html>bikkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikkels.html>bikkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bikkel.html>bikkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:talus.html>talus</a>, a bone in a sheep's <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></li>
<li>such a bone (often worked and) used as in a dice-like game of chance</li>
<li>any artificial, similar throwing device; a <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></li>
<li>pebble</li>
<li>robust, resilient person</li>
<li>pickaxe</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***bil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bil.html>bil</a> (8763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bille</i>, often used in compounds, borrowed from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ingvaeonic" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ingvaeonic">Ingvaeonic</a>/<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Sea_Germanic" class="extiw" title="w:North Sea Germanic">North Sea</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und">*<a href = vnd.unilang:belle.html>belle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balliō-</i>, a variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balluz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bil.html>bil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:billetje.html>billetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A buttock, <i>usually used in the plural: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a></b>, unless specified as left/right</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bíþla-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, instrumental noun from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bītaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>However, compare <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bilją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blade, axe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which could have influenced its development.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bil.html>bil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:billetje.html>billetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a hammer-like double-edged tool used by stonecutters and <a href = vnd.unilang:millers.html>millers</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bilhamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zwaaispits</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tweespits</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">biller</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">steenbiller</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bilhamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bilmachine</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
